## Legal Interpretation Summary:
### Subject: Will of Roland Ross Womack, Jr. ‚Äì Executor Authority & Beneficiary Limits

**Document Reviewed**: Last Will and Testament of Roland Ross Womack, Jr.  
**Execution Date**: May 21, 2010  
**Executor Named**: Nancy Faye Womack (spouse)  
**Beneficiaries Named**: Nancy Faye Womack (spouse), Phyllis Charlene Usry (daughter), Ethan Ross Womack (son)

---

### A. Executor Authority (Sections I.1‚ÄìI.3)

The will authorizes Nancy Faye Womack, as executor:

- To administer the estate without court bond, appraisals, or returns.  
- To sell, transfer, and convey estate property at public or private sale.  
- To execute transfers without court order, holding proceeds in trust per will instructions.

**Crucially**: These powers are administrative only. They do **not** permit changes to the designated beneficiaries or the proportions of inheritance.

---

### B. Beneficiary Structure (Sections D‚ÄìG)

**If Nancy Faye Womack survives Roland Ross Womack** (Section E):
- She is to receive *all* of the rest, residue, and remainder of the estate.

**If she does not survive him** (Section F):
- The estate is to be divided *equally* between his children:
  - Phyllis Charlene Usry
  - Ethan Ross Womack

**In the event that either child does not survive him**, their share is to go to their issue (i.e., their children), per stirpes.

**There is no provision in the will that allows Faye to redirect, restructure, or exclude Ethan Ross Womack** or to convert assets for exclusive control.

---

### C. Division of Personal Effects (Section D)

If Faye survives:
- She inherits all personal effects.

If not:
- Executor is directed to divide items *equitably* between children (or their issue).
- If children cannot agree, executor may divide them ‚Äúas my executor(s) may deem equitable.‚Äù

**This is a logistical directive, not a redistribution power**.

---

### Conclusion:

Nancy Faye Womack was **empowered to administer** the estate‚Äînot to change its structure. Any act that excludes or minimizes Ethan Ross Womack‚Äôs rightful share under this will may constitute:

- Breach of fiduciary duty as executor
- Intentional disinheritance not authorized by the testator
- Possible fraudulent conveyance or misappropriation of estate assets

This will should serve as the **foundational document for estate claims** made by Ethan Ross Womack as a legal heir.

2025-06-07T22:01:42.686005Z ‚Äî user

I can‚Äôt send the file it‚Äôs too large - how do I use terminal to upload to my bucket?

2025-06-07T22:01:44.103730Z ‚Äî assistant

Perfect ‚Äî using your Cloudflare R2 bucket via the terminal is exactly the right move. Here‚Äôs how to upload your full archive (chat exports, images, etc.) to your bucket using the terminal. This guide assumes you're on macOS or Linux, but it works similarly on Windows with PowerShell.

üõ†Ô∏è Step-by-Step: Upload Files to Your R2 Bucket via Terminal

1. Install the AWS CLI (if not already installed)

Cloudflare R2 is S3-compatible, so you'll use the AWS CLI.

brew install awscli    # macOS (use appropriate method for Linux or Windows)

Verify it's installed:

aws --version

2. Get Your R2 Credentials from Cloudflare

Go to:

Cloudflare Dashboard ‚Üí R2 ‚Üí Manage R2 API Tokens

You'll need: - Access Key ID - Secret Access Key - Bucket Name (e.g. womack-case) - Account ID - R2 Endpoint (e.g. https://<accountid>.r2.cloudflarestorage.com)

3. Configure the AWS CLI for Cloudflare R2

Run:

aws configure --profile cloudflare-r2

And enter:

AWS Access Key ID [None]: <your-access-key>
AWS Secret Access Key [None]: <your-secret-key>
Default region name [None]: auto
Default output format [None]: json

Now create a file in your home directory to tell AWS how to talk to R2:

nano ~/.aws/config

Paste this:

[profile cloudflare-r2]
region = auto
s3 =
  endpoint_url = https://<your-account-id>.r2.cloudflarestorage.com

Save and exit (CTRL+X, Y, Enter)

4. Upload Files to the R2 Bucket

aws s3 cp /path/to/your/folder s3://womack-case/ --recursive --profile cloudflare-r2

Examples:

aws s3 cp ~/Documents/Womack_Case_File s3://womack-case/ --recursive --profile cloudflare-r2

You can also upload individual files:

aws s3 cp chat_export.zip s3://womack-case/ --profile cloudflare-r2

‚úÖ Bonus: Generate a Shareable Link

If your bucket is public, files will be accessible at:

https://<accountid>.r2.cloudflarestorage.com/womack-case/<filename>

If it's private, you can generate pre-signed URLs (let me know if you want that script).

Once it‚Äôs up, send me the link or confirm it‚Äôs uploaded ‚Äî and I‚Äôll begin indexing and assembling the archive structure around it.

Want me to generate an upload.sh script for you that automates this?

How do I just use my aws bucket

2025-06-07T22:02:26.985191Z ‚Äî assistant

Great ‚Äî if you already have a regular AWS S3 bucket (not Cloudflare R2), the process is simpler and more standardized. Here‚Äôs how to upload files using your AWS S3 bucket from the terminal:

‚úÖ Step-by-Step: Upload Files to AWS S3 from Terminal

üîß 1. Install AWS CLI (if not already installed)

macOS:

brew install awscli

Ubuntu/Debian:

sudo apt install awscli

Windows:
Install from: https://aws.amazon.com/cli/

üîê 2. Configure Your AWS CLI

Run:

aws configure

Then enter:

AWS Access Key ID [None]: <your-access-key-id>
AWS Secret Access Key [None]: <your-secret-access-key>
Default region name [None]: us-east-1         # or whatever your bucket's region is
Default output format [None]: json

This will save your credentials locally in ~/.aws/credentials.

ü™£ 3. Upload a File to Your S3 Bucket

To upload a single file:

aws s3 cp /path/to/file.txt s3://your-bucket-name/

To upload a whole folder:

aws s3 cp /path/to/folder s3://your-bucket-name/ --recursive

üìÇ 4. Example Upload Commands

aws s3 cp ./case-evidence.zip s3://womack-case-archive/

aws s3 cp ./photos/ s3://womack-case-archive/photos/ --recursive

üåç 5. Accessing the File

If your bucket is public, files can be accessed at:

https://your-bucket-name.s3.amazonaws.com/filename.ext

If it‚Äôs private, you can generate a temporary pre-signed URL:

aws s3 presign s3://your-bucket-name/filename.ext --expires-in 3600

That link will be valid for 1 hour.

Want a script you can double-click to re-upload everything? Let me know your upload folder path, and I‚Äôll generate a shell script for you.
